The Abyssinian Question: A Major Upheaval - British Foreign Secretary Hoare Resigns - Baldwin Rumored to Concurrently Hold Foreign Secretary Post - French Political Situation Also on the Verge of Change 40

London - British Foreign Secretary Sir Samuel Hoare has resigned and the government has not attempted to retain him. Although official circles have not yet stated the reason for his resignation, it is widely believed to be due to widespread opposition in Britain and elsewhere to the peace plan he and French Prime Minister Laval formulated in Paris. Hoare intends to complete his questioning in the House of Commons today and, as a member of Parliament, provide a personal explanation. No successor has been determined for the Foreign Secretary post at present. It is rumored that Prime Minister Baldwin will concurrently hold the post, or that Chancellor of the Exchequer Chamberlain will be transferred to head the Foreign Office. The House of Commons hopes the new Foreign Secretary will be a truly great figure. If Chamberlain does head the Foreign Office, supporters of the government will be greatly satisfied, and the situation could become calmer, as even opponents of the government would feel somewhat relieved by Chamberlain's leadership. It is said that if Chamberlain is transferred to head the Foreign Office, the position of Chancellor of the Exchequer might be given to Churchill. It is reported that Hoare resigned at 6:30 PM last night, deciding to take a six-month rest. At a time when the situation is increasingly tense, Hoare's departure could make the government's position slightly easier, but the turmoil has not subsided. Supporters of the government feel they have no way to face the nation after last week's events, and there is a strong sense that the government will be reorganized. In any case, the important debate on the peace plan in the House of Commons today has been altered by Hoare's resignation. It is now heard that Conservative MP Winterton will move an amendment to the Labour Party's impeachment motion. According to reliable sources, this amendment states that the House of Commons, on the one hand, recognizes that any solution to the Italo-Abyssinian dispute must be acceptable to the League of Nations, and on the other hand, is willing to fully support the government in carrying out the foreign policy stated in its manifesto and approved by the people in the general election. Hoare had prepared a 4,000-word explanation to be delivered during today's debate, but it is widely believed that as his remarks are now personal, their scope may not be as broad. It is heard that Hoare believes the amendment proposed by Parliament is tantamount to impeaching him personally, which is also one of the reasons for his resignation. Hoare is 52 years old and has served in politics since the age of 25. In early June of this year, during a cabinet reshuffle, Hoare was transferred from the position of Secretary of State for India to head the Foreign Office, having served for just over six months. (Reuters, 19th)

Paris - According to reliable French sources, the resignation of British Foreign Secretary Hoare will have an impact that makes the positions of French Prime Minister Laval even more precarious. Laval only received a majority of 54 votes in the Chamber of Deputies yesterday, which could not be considered satisfactory. It is widely expected that if another vote is held tomorrow, hundreds of votes will shift away from yesterday's support. Some quarters believe that Laval may follow in Hoare's footsteps, and will inevitably fail in the Chamber of Deputies next week. (Reuters, 19th)

Paris - It is rumored that following the sudden resignation of former British Foreign Secretary Hoare and the resignation of Hervé, Minister without Portfolio, from the leadership of the Radical Socialist Party, Prime Minister and Foreign Minister Laval may also resign. Pessimistic views are quite prevalent in the lobbies of the Chamber of Deputies. (Havas, 19th)

Paris - It is widely believed that Hervé's action is the prelude to the collapse of the Laval cabinet. The general opinion is that if a new cabinet is formed and a suitable figure cannot be found to take the helm, Hervé, despite his previous statement that he would not form another cabinet, can still be expected to accept the position. Hervé's cabinet would be extremely pro-British, supportive of the League of Nations, and would assist the Emperor of Abyssinia in opposing Italy. (Reuters, 19th)

Fierce Debate in the British House of Commons - Hoare Calmly Explains 41

Compromise Focused on Maintaining Anglo-French Unity - As Many As 200 MPs Asked Questions

London - Hoare, who resigned as Foreign Secretary this morning, explained the process of drafting the peace plan in his personal capacity during the debate on the peace plan in the House of Commons this afternoon. Hoare entered the House of Commons to cheers from the government party, sitting quietly in a corner of the chamber. At 3:46 PM, Hoare, in calm and clear language, asked the House of Commons to be patient, as the matter was very complex and had special difficulties. He said that he had gone abroad for medical advice and had been injured in a fall, preventing him from immediately returning to handle the issue, which led to misunderstandings and criticisms. Now that misunderstandings have taken root, it is very difficult to defend himself. Since taking office as Foreign Secretary, he felt that there were two major issues of urgent necessity: 1. To exert his utmost ability to prevent the spread of war in Europe; 2. To prevent a separate war between Britain and Italy. The government has received reports from various sources stating that Italy would consider an oil embargo as a military sanction, or would take action to declare war on Italy. No matter what threats Italy poses, we are determined not to fear them. If Italy attacks us, we should retaliate. Historically, we have always retaliated against those who offend us, and achieved complete victory. But we have a concept in mind that such a separate attack on one country, without the full assistance of other countries, would inevitably lead to the division of the League of Nations. The Paris peace plan is the minimum basis for the French government to proceed. He himself was dissatisfied with several specific points of this plan, but he felt that the matter was of great importance, and the continuation of the Italo-Abyssinian War was even more serious, so he recognized that the matter was worth trying, as maintaining Anglo-French unity was a necessity. We are now entering a more dangerous stage. Apart from the British fleet in the Mediterranean, and the additional deployment of troops to Egypt, Malta, and Aden, no other member states of the League of Nations have sent a single ship or mobilized a single soldier. During the House of Commons session, the public gallery was extremely crowded, and as many as 200 MPs asked questions. Debate arose in the chamber, causing many answers to be inaudible. The Speaker had to repeatedly intervene to restore order. (Reuters, 19th)

A Major Change in British Politics - Varying Rumors Regarding the Reasons for Hoare's Resignation 42

London - The sudden resignation of British Foreign Secretary Hoare has had a profound impact on official circles here, who believe it is the most shocking event in British politics since 1914. People in France are undoubtedly shocked, as this event is sufficient to greatly affect the compromise recently reached in Paris between Britain and France on the Italo-Abyssinian issue. During Hoare's negotiations in Paris, he consistently demonstrated his superior insight, courageous spirit, and the merits of being practical and unpretentious, with concentrated focus, which was praised by people in France. It is generally believed that Italian Prime Minister Mussolini's speech at the inauguration ceremony of the new village of Pontinia in that country yesterday made Hoare feel embarrassed, and thus he could not avoid resigning. In short, this move will inevitably have a profound impact on the situation of the League of Nations General Assembly's current discussion of the Italo-Abyssinian dispute in the short term, and its significance is by no means ordinary. (Havas, 19th)

London - The Foreign Secretary telegraphed his resignation today. Some days ago, various parties had anticipated this, but yesterday the news suddenly shifted to the belief that a cabinet crisis had been avoided, and Hoare would not need to resign. The reason for Hoare's resignation is probably that there were too many opponents to the peace plan he and French Prime Minister and Foreign Minister Laval had drafted, and the published White Paper mentioned that Hoare had instructed the British Ambassador to Italy to strongly urge the Abyssinian Emperor to accept the plan, reaching the peak of opposition. Some in the House of Commons even called this action "shameful." At the same time, Prime Minister Baldwin spoke in the House of Commons today, stating that the French government had assured Britain that if Italy attacked the British fleet in the Mediterranean, France would back Britain. This assurance has long been known to everyone, but it is only now being publicly confirmed in the House of Commons. The Associated Press also learned from reliable sources that Hoare's resignation was actually due to disagreements within the cabinet over the draft of his speech to the House of Commons on Thursday. It is understood that Hoare wanted to make every effort to defend his actions, while Chancellor of the Exchequer Chamberlain wanted Hoare to admit his mistakes. Therefore, Hoare's resignation was deeply surprising even to Baldwin, but he accepted it shortly afterward. The selection of a successor has not yet been determined today. All parties believe that Eden is the most experienced. Sir Eric Drummond also intends to resign due to several months of illness. It is said that Hoare himself deeply felt that Eden had not provided assistance in Geneva, so he had no choice but to resign. (National News, 18th)

London - Sir Samuel Hoare, the Foreign Secretary, has submitted his resignation to Prime Minister Baldwin, resulting in a change in the British political situation. Italian Prime Minister Mussolini delivered a speech at the new village of Pontinia this morning, in which he said, "All the selfish and hypocritical people in the world have come out to oppose us. We are determined to deal with them with generosity and passion, and victory will ultimately belong to us." These words were clearly directed at the British people. After hearing this speech, the British Conservative Party was extremely indignant, and the political turmoil suddenly intensified. The Foreign Secretary then also decided to resign. It is generally believed that after the Foreign Secretary resigns, the target of all attacks will no longer exist, and the government will easily gain the support of a majority of MPs when it attends the House of Commons tomorrow. (Havas, 18th)

Cadogan or Rose Rumored to be Appointed Undersecretary of State for Foreign Affairs in Britain 43

London - Since the resignation of former Foreign Secretary Hoare, the senior official in the Foreign Office, Sir Eric Drummond, immediately followed suit and submitted his resignation. To date, the government has made every effort to retain him, but political circles believe that the government will probably approve his resignation. After his departure, Sir Alexander Cadogan, the Ambassador to China; Sir Ronald Lindsay, the Ambassador to the United States; Sir Miles Lampson, the High Commissioner to Egypt; and Sir Leith-Ross, who is currently investigating financial and monetary conditions in China, are all hoping to succeed as Undersecretary of State for Foreign Affairs. (Havas, 19th)

British Newspapers Mostly Express Sympathy for Hoare's Resignation - Believing He Maintained Good Demeanor - Baldwin in a Dilemma 44

London - The Times stated in its editorial today that there is a honorable custom in British political circles that any cabinet member who is closely related to a failed strategy must resign. Now, Foreign Secretary Hoare's resignation is in accordance with this custom. Hoare was implicated for failing to prevent an indefensible proposal, and should be sympathized with by the general public. The government should regard today's debate on the peace plan as an opportunity to explain the reasons for its actions and to soothe people's hearts. This newspaper believes that the process of restoring British policy and prestige should begin from now on. The Daily Telegraph editorial said that Hoare's resignation is a sad interruption in a very promising career, but the public recognizes Hoare's resignation as a normal course of action, as this peace plan is criticized from all sides. The resignation of the Foreign Secretary will hardly reduce the seriousness of today's debate. The Morning Post stated that Hoare's resignation is of course intended to ease the serious situation for which he should be responsible, but Hoare is only a tool of the policy for which both the British and French governments should be responsible. The Daily Mirror stated that if Hoare's resignation can strengthen Baldwin's position, it would not be surprising. The people will listen to his speech in the House of Commons today with sympathy and attention. The Daily Express stated that Hoare's resignation is a victory for the left-wing Conservatives. Baldwin surrendered without a fight, offering Hoare as a sacrifice to the opposition party. However, it is difficult to understand why the helmsman has fallen into the sea, while the captain is still in office. The Daily Mail stated that Hoare is taking the blame for others, and the situation will be chaotic and uncertain due to his resignation. The Daily News stated that Hoare's resignation can help restore British prestige, but the Prime Minister has hardly escaped the dilemma of being in a difficult position, and has failed to overthrow a colleague to restore the cabinet's credibility, and this colleague's speech on the Italo-Abyssinian dispute at the League of Nations General Assembly greatly contributed to the Prime Minister's victory in the general election. The Daily Express stated that the method of having two foreign ministers and two foreign policies has plunged us into a situation of disaster and humiliation. It is hoped that from now on there will be one foreign minister and one foreign policy based on the League of Nations. The Manchester Guardian stated that the issue now is the origin of the peace plan. Although Hoare has now resigned, the government cannot shirk the responsibility of explaining this matter in detail. The Liverpool Daily Post stated that Hoare's resignation was almost inevitable, but it is also very regrettable, as Hoare had gained a good reputation before negotiating the peace, and was considered a talented foreign minister. Eden is already in Geneva, we recognize his policies, and Hoare had no choice but to resign for the sake of dignity. The Nottingham Daily Express stated that the British government has repeatedly failed to weaken its resolve regarding the aspirations of French politicians, resulting in the underestimation of British policy. The Berkshire Observer stated that British politics should not be suspected of being dominated by French influence. (Reuters, 19th)

Radical Party Leader Hervé Also Resigns 45

And Will Withdraw From Cabinet

Paris - Hervé, the Minister without Portfolio and former Prime Minister, has resigned from the leadership of the Radical Socialist Party today. Informed observers expect the cabinet to resign, as Hervé is clearly no longer able to make all the members of the Radical Socialist Party support Laval. Some party members believe that the party can be divided into two factions, one still led by Hervé, and the other supporting former Prime Minister Daladier. Those who are friendly with the government have also admitted today that a cabinet crisis may occur. Before Hervé resigned, he gave a speech at a meeting of his party, during which some people shouted "Stop this farce." Hervé also rebuked party members, saying that they had first supported the peace plan, but in the Chamber of Deputies, the majority voted against it. "I cannot both lead a political party that attacks the government and be a member of the government," so he suddenly said. (National News, 18th)

Paris - The Executive Committee of the Radical Socialist Party met last night to discuss the government's policy on the Italo-Abyssinian dispute, which immediately led to fierce debate. There were many speakers, and the debate lasted for a long time. As a result of the debate, Hervé, the Minister without Portfolio, finally resigned from the leadership of the party. Previously, all the members of the Executive Committee, except for five who expressed dissent, unanimously passed a motion advocating that the party's position be made concrete. Unexpectedly, as soon as the motion was passed, Vidal, a left-wing fighter of the party, stood up and spoke, vehemently attacking Hervé in his personal capacity, saying that he should not collude with the government, disregard the League of Nations Covenant, and willingly be deceived by Prime Minister Laval. Hervé was very indignant when he heard this, and immediately announced his resignation from the leadership of the party to the Committee. Although the Committee strongly urged him to stay, Hervé's intention to resign remained firm until this morning. (Havas, 19th)

Paris - Hervé, the leader of the Radical Socialist Party and Minister without Portfolio, has resigned from his position as party leader. Recently, there have been rumors that Hervé expressed dissatisfaction with the Italo-Abyssinian dispute resolution plan proposed by Britain and France, and was considering the issue of his continued service. Later, his attitude became more moderate, apparently striving to avoid a cabinet crisis. Until yesterday, when the Chamber of Deputies discussed the foreign ministry's budget and voted on a motion of confidence in the government, only more than forty members of the Radical Socialist Party voted in favor, while more than eighty voted against it. In this situation, Hervé had only two paths to follow: one was to resign and cause political disputes, and the other was to resign as party leader to apologize to the party. Finally, because the internal and external affairs were at a critical juncture, not allowing for any changes, he resolutely resigned as party leader to preserve the overall situation. (Havas, 18th)

Paris - Hervé, the leader of the Radical Socialist Party, also hinted that he might withdraw from the cabinet. Hervé is the son of a gendarmerie officer, from a poor family, and is now sixty-three years old. He has held the premiership three times, and his tireless efforts are highly respected by the people. (Reuters, 19th)

Fascist Party Leadership to Convene Again Today 46

Due to Complications Arising from British Foreign Secretary's Resignation

Rome - The Supreme Council of the Fascist Party held a meeting last night that lasted a very long time. No resolution was made regarding the Paris peace plan. According to the Il Giornale d'Italia, after studying the political situation related to the peace conditions, the Council decided to postpone the meeting until December 20. The postponement of the Council's meeting is widely believed to be due to the resignation of British Foreign Secretary Hoare, which has made international affairs confusing and uncertain. Because the Council is still unclear about what policies the British government will adopt in the future, it believes that it is appropriate to wait until the British House of Commons debates foreign policy today before holding another meeting to discuss everything. People in Italy all believe that Hoare's resignation and the reasons for his resignation have greatly reversed the progress of the peace talks. (Reuters, 19th)

Rome - The Supreme Council of the Fascist Party met at the Palazzo Venezia at 10 PM last night, chaired by Prime Minister Mussolini. At the beginning of the meeting, Mussolini paid tribute to General De Bono, the former High Commissioner to East Africa, saying, "De Bono's name will be inscribed in history alongside the recovery of the cities of Adowa and Magdala," etc. The Supreme Council is now scheduled to continue the meeting on the 20th. After adjourning today, a brief communique was issued stating that "The Supreme Council of the Fascist Party studied the political situation generated by the Italo-Abyssinian dispute resolution plan proposed by Britain and France," etc. These few words were not considered unusual by the general public. Official circles said that those who participated in the meeting today were all senior officials, which shows that the Council must have studied the possibility of Italy's long-term resistance to sanctions. It was also said that the government's foreign policy will definitely announce its outline before the end of the current session of the Supreme Council of the Fascist Party. Regarding the speech delivered by British Minister without Portfolio Eden at the Executive Council of the League of Nations yesterday, and the resignation of British Foreign Secretary Hoare, and the resignation of Hervé, the French Minister without Portfolio, from the leadership of the Radical Socialist Party, officials here believe that these are major events, and that the changes in the European balance of power can be seen here. (Havas, 19th)

New York - It was learned today that Italy has established bank credit here in order to purchase more than 100,000 tons of scrap copper. Calculated at the current price, the total amount of the credit should be more than 1.3 million. (Reuters, 19th)

Emperor of Abyssinia Replies to League of Nations - Believes Britain and France Have No Right to Overstep Their Bounds and Act on His Behalf 47

Geneva - The official reply of the Emperor of Abyssinia regarding the peace plan proposed by Britain and France was recently delivered to the Secretariat of the League of Nations by the country's representative, Gedamu Wald. The content briefly stated that "Regarding the peace plan, no responsible body of the League of Nations has entrusted anyone to draft it, and to submit the draft to the countries concerned." It also stated that the Executive Council of the League of Nations has already reserved the right to mediate. Moreover, when French Prime Minister Laval and British Foreign Secretary Hoare conducted negotiations, the Abyssinian government was not invited to express its views. The Abyssinian government had previously sent a note to the British government, explaining the principles that should be followed in resolving the dispute. Later, before this plan was sent to his country, he requested the French government to meet with his country's ambassador to France, and also requested to obtain this plan, which should be clearly announced by the League of Nations as not in line with the various principles of the Covenant. (Havas, 18th)

Thirteen-Nation Committee Resolves to Reject British-French Plan - Declares Seeking a Basis for Peace Talks Futile - Resolution Immediately Presented to League of Nations Executive Council 49

Geneva - Today, the Executive Council of the League of Nations held a meeting of the thirteen-member committee for two hours, unanimously passing a brief resolution on the British-French peace plan. The content has not been released, but it is heard that the resolution firmly declares that the British-French attempt to seek a basis for resolving the Italo-Abyssinian War has proven futile. Thus, the plan has been effectively rejected. The resolution also proposes that the thirteen-nation committee should reconvene when the development of the situation requires further study. The resolution of the thirteen-nation committee will be submitted to the League of Nations Executive Council shortly. (Reuters, 19th)

League of Nations Personnel: From Disappointment to Excitement; Britain and France Declare the Result of Frankness 50

Geneva – The representatives of Britain and France attending the League of Nations Council today stated that they were prepared to abandon the peace plan if the League of Nations could not fully endorse it. The British Minister without Portfolio, Eden, said that the two countries always intended that the plan should be approved by the League of Nations. The French Prime Minister and Foreign Minister, Laval, sent a letter to the Council requesting that it modify or reject the parts of the plan that it did not approve. He believed that if the League of Nations could not accept the entire plan, it should continue to strive for a "reasonable and fair solution." After receiving Laval's letter, the Council announced an adjournment, but it may hold a secret meeting tomorrow to allow the countries to express their criticisms. The Albanian Minister to France and representative to the League of Nations, Marian, delivered a lengthy speech today, declaring that Albania would never accept a peace plan that involved the colonization of its territory. Thus, the peace plan of Britain and France has apparently become a thing of the past, and the League of Nations representatives can only figure out how to dispose of its remains. (18th National Telegram)

Geneva – Yesterday, after the British representative Eden and the French Prime Minister Laval spoke at the League of Nations Council meeting, the view that the Paris peace plan, initially embraced in Geneva in early November, was dead was confirmed. As a result, the mood shifted from disappointment to excitement. The two statesmen's speeches were quite short, both stating that if the plan could not satisfy the wishes of the members of the Council, they were willing to abandon it. It is expected that when the League of Nations Council holds a closed meeting today, the representatives of the Soviet Union, Spain, and Denmark will all deliver important speeches, but they will not launch unrestrained attacks, as the plan has now been abandoned. However, it is felt that if the Italian government's reply to the peace plan indicates acceptance, Laval will definitely oppose extending sanctions against Italy to oil and other key commodities. During yesterday's Council meeting, Eden spoke first, recalling that the Sanctions Adjustment Committee had endorsed the attempt to find a basis for discussion between Italy and Abyssinia. He then spoke of the efforts of the British and French governments to create the Paris plan, saying that the two governments had a crucial condition in mind, namely, that the terms of peace should be subject to the League's approval, before being imposed on Italy and Abyssinia. All League members were bound to respect and strive to fulfill the obligations of the League Covenant. The task the two governments had undertaken was not easy, and given the current turn of events, almost impossible. Nevertheless, they had to try their best. He could not apologize for this. Even if this attempt did not succeed, the goal of reconciliation remained, and this should be recognized by the League. Therefore, even if the plan could not be implemented at present, its principles were justified. Eden went on to say that the peace plan was not presented as something unchangeable. It was presented in order to learn the views of all parties involved in the dispute. Therefore, if the plan now before the meeting did not contain essential conditions acceptable to all three parties, the British government could not continue to apply for or support it. It was the British government's view that this particular attempt to resolve the dispute was not even close to achieving its goal, so the British government did not wish to continue it.

Laval spoke, expressing great sympathy for the spirit in which the two governments had drawn up the peace plan. He went on to say that he did not know how Italy and Abyssinia would respond to their proposal. He suggested that the Council avoid making a firm decision before receiving the Italian and Abyssinian replies. However, he felt that he should announce at this time that if this attempt could not obtain the support of the parties concerned, the Council should decide on its own and not disregard any honest method based on world peace.

Before the Council adjourned, the only other speaker was the Abyssinian representative, Mayang, who said that the Abyssinian government had submitted the Italo-Abyssinian dispute to the League of Nations and believed that it would be resolved in accordance with the principles and spirit of the League Covenant. The League Covenant must be respected, and Abyssinia could not accept a peace treaty of surrender or plunder. He did not believe that the League of Nations would abandon Abyssinia and hand it over to a brutal enemy. The only civilization Italy had given was incendiary bombs. Mayang then asked whether it was in accordance with the principles of the Covenant to force the victim of aggression to acknowledge the ceding of territory to the aggressor and to allow it to control more territory. Abyssinia had placed its own fate in the hands of the Council and reserved the right to present its views later.

The Chairman then announced an indefinite adjournment, saying that until the attitudes of Italy and Abyssinia were clear, the members of the League of Nations would naturally wish to wait for the meeting to reconvene to study the issue. (19th Reuters Telegram)

Geneva – The resignation of British Foreign Secretary Hoare is creating a stir here today. This news, along with the complete failure of the British-French peace plan, has increased hopes for the effectiveness of sanctions against Italy, and the oil embargo may soon be put to a vote. (18th National Press Telegram)

Geneva – There is shock and confusion here at the news of the resignation of British Foreign Secretary Hoare. Hoare made a very good impression when he attended the League of Nations General Assembly in September. It is felt that Hoare's diplomatic experience was still insufficient, and he was unable to handle the extreme difficulties of this international event properly. However, his ability to retreat from difficulty is a sign of his sincerity. The Abyssinian delegation openly admitted that they welcomed this news. Hoare's resignation is proof that Britain will resolutely uphold the principles of the League of Nations and its Covenant, and ensure that the Italo-Abyssinian dispute is resolved in accordance with these principles. (19th Reuters Telegram)

The World's Silver Market Center: Transfer from London to New York 54

London – Although the price of large silver bars here today was one and seven-eighths pence lower than yesterday, the U.S. Treasury Department is still unwilling to purchase them. It is said that this is another step in the transfer of the world's silver market from London to New York. The silver prices in London and New York are still not equal, and this could make New York a better market for selling silver. (18th Reuters Telegram)

New York – Today, the Hand Harman Chamber of Commerce broke the custom of the New York silver market by publishing silver prices before receiving reports from the London market. This is because the Treasury Department is buying in the Mound City market and selling in New York. The near-term Mound City silver market is higher than the far-term market, which is also why. Although Treasury Secretary Morgenthau has repeatedly stated that he will not abandon the silver purchase plan, it is generally believed that if this continues, the U.S. government will inevitably stop purchasing silver in foreign markets. (18th Electric Current Telegram)

Bombay – At a meeting of the Bombay Large Silver Bar Exchange Council, someone proposed reducing the minimum price for futures trading. This proposal was not passed. Spot trading is temporarily suspended until Sunday. It is reported that there were few transactions when the market price was around 52 rupees and a half. Banks now require a guarantee deposit of at least 25 percent for large silver bars. (15th Reuters Telegram)

Washington – U.S. Senate silver faction senators disagreed today on the continued decline in silver prices. The Thomas faction, which has always advocated raising the silver price to $1.29 per ounce as soon as possible, believes that the continued decline in silver prices is harmful. However, the Pittman faction believes that the decline in silver prices is not a cause for concern. Apparently, speculators in London, who had hoped for a silver price of 65 cents per ounce last week, were disappointed and no longer concerned about the market price, and engaged in dumping silver. The Pittman faction believes that the United States will continue to purchase silver, regardless of London market dumping of 10 million ounces. However, those who remain silent observers at the Treasury Department believe that the silver faction will still be confused after Congress convenes in January next year. However, if this faction can unite in the face of continued decline in silver prices, the situation will change again. (18th National Press Telegram)

Ministry of Finance Revises Diesel Tax Rules 62

Nanjing – The Ministry of Finance reported that batches of diesel imported through Xiamen, Hankou, and other places were tested and found to have a specific gravity and ignition point that matched the Grade A diesel tax rules, but the kerosene content was as high as 80% or more. Although the quality was inferior, after import, it could be used for ignition without refining. It was obviously specially manufactured to apply the low tax rate for Grade A diesel on the one hand and to sell it as kerosene without refining on the other, in order to make a large profit. In order to protect kerosene customs duties, it is necessary to prevent the continued import of this specially made diesel. The Executive Yuan has approved the revision of the Grade A clause of the diesel tax rules in Article 529 of the current import tariff, which will be implemented on New Year's Day next year, and has ordered the Director-General of Customs and customs supervisors to comply. (19th Central News Agency Telegram)

Zhang Honglie Telegram to Nanjing: Report on Dongzhuang Embankment Work 76

Nanjing – Zhang Honglie, the Director of the Yellow River Dongzhuang Embankment Work in Shandong Province, telegraphed the National Economic Council to report on the work. 1. The Lisheng Tunlitou project has completed the construction of 32 dam barriers with stones and 23 with wickerwork, plus the repair of 5 wickerwork dams. 2. The Jiangsu Houxin Dike has moved about 185,000 cubic meters of earth, completing 80% of the work, with 2,000 workers daily. 3. The Jiangsu Baquan Dike project has moved 75,000 cubic meters of earth, completing 70% of the work, with 880 workers daily. 4. The construction of dams for the four breach points (234) has continued. The total length of the four dams is 1,170 meters, only 160 meters shorter than the design. However, it is not possible to guide the river flow, and it may be necessary to extend them in the future. 5. The Jiangsu Ba Xin dams (1, 2, 4) and Jiu dams (3, 4, 5, 6) have all been protected with stones and extended to cover the breach mouth by ten dams. 6. The construction of the protection for the material factories and small embankments covers approximately 78,800 feet of land and is 70% complete, with 200 workers daily. 7. The formal flow measured on each day of December was 1,151 cubic meters per second, and the flow in the old river was 11 cubic meters per second, accounting for 1% of the total river flow. (19th Special Telegram)

Japan Increases Troops Stationed in North China, Kita and Muto Reach Agreement in Tianjin, Implementation Expected One Month After Approval 92

Tianjin News: Colonel Kita Seiichi, Chief of the China Section of the Japanese General Staff Headquarters, and Lieutenant Colonel Muto Akira, Chief of the Manchuria Group, arrived in Tanggu from Dalian on the Tianjin Maru on the morning of the 13th of this month, carrying orders from their military headquarters. At noon, they took the Beining Railway to Tianjin. Chief of Staff Sakai of the garrison army, senior staff officers Ishii, staff officers Nakai, Doeki, senior adjutant Otake, section members Hayashi, and Iida all welcomed them at the East Station. After getting off the train, they stayed at the Yamato Hotel in the Japanese Concession. Chen Yi and Li Zeyi happened to be in Tianjin and visited them at noon to discuss the North China situation. In the afternoon, around 2 PM, Kita and Muto visited Commander Tada at the Zhangyuan Commander's Residence and held a meeting focusing on the North China incident. Besides Tada, Kita, and Muto, those present included Sakai, Takeshita, Takahashi, Ishino (military attaché in Jinan), Otake, Ishii, Doeki, and Colonel Hasegawa, the commander of the Beijing unit of the North China Garrison Army, Colonel Kayashima, the commander of the Tianjin unit, Lieutenant Colonel Kagawa, the commander of the Tanggu unit, Major Nakajima, the commander of the Qinhuangdao-Yushuguan unit, and Major Onii, the commander of the Tangshan unit, totaling more than 20 people. Kita and Muto conveyed the central intentions of the military headquarters, and Sakai, Takahashi, and Takeshita reported on the recent situation in North China. After 3 PM, they discussed the reorganization of the North China Garrison Army and a plan to increase its strength. A principle decision was made at that time. That evening, Tada hosted a banquet at his official residence. After 9 AM on the 14th, Tada again summoned Kita, Muto, and the commanders of the various garrison units to discuss the budget and troop numbers for expanding the North China Garrison Army. After half a day of discussion, it was decided to increase the number of troops to around 3,000 to 2,400. In addition to Beijing, Tianjin, Tanggu, Tangshan, Qinhuangdao, Yushuguan, Zhangjiakou, Fushun, and Le, it is also planned to station a small number of soldiers in Tongxian and Ninghe, on the border of the war zone, for the purpose of protecting the peace and security of the war zone and for liaison purposes. The budget is being rushed to be compiled, and Lieutenant Colonel Muto will take it back after returning from Beijing to submit it to the military headquarters for review and approval in advance. It is expected to be implemented in January of next year. However, it is still undecided whether the troops will be transferred from Japan or whether a portion will be transferred from the Kwantung Army to be under the command of the North China Garrison Army. Kita and Muto took the Beining Railway to Beijing on the 15th to visit Song Zheyuan and others to observe the future trends of the North China situation. They are scheduled to take a plane to Chengde on the 20th to meet the commander of the 7th Division, and then transfer to Changchun to meet Commander Nanjirō. They will return to Japan by land on the 25th. Muto plans to leave Beijing on the 18th and return to Tianjin, then take a train out of the pass and return to Japan via Korea. The new Chief of Staff of the North China Garrison Army is Colonel Nagami Gotoku, a senior advisor to the military administration of the puppet Manchukuo, who is scheduled to come to Tianjin on the 17th with the new section member of the North China Garrison Army, Major Hamada Hiroshi, to take over their duties. The former Chief of Staff, Sakai, had already been ordered to return to the General Staff Headquarters in his country. However, because he is familiar with the situation in North China, he has been retained for two months to handle special affairs. The newly appointed Staff Officer Hamada will assist him in handling these matters. The Navy, which will coordinate with the expansion of the garrison army, has already established a naval port office in Tianjin by Captain Kubota, the former staff officer of the Ryojun Naval Port. The office is located in the Mitsui Bussan Kaisha in the Japanese Concession and has already begun operations. When necessary, the office can directly command the ships of the 14th Destroyer Division of the 3rd Overseas Fleet. The ships of the 14th Destroyer Division, the Hagi and Aoi, are docked in Tanggu, and the Kiku is docked at the Tianjin Special First District Wharf, with no intention of leaving for the time being. In addition, seven planes are still parked at the Nankai Balitai Airfield in Tianjin. Although they have not taken off recently, there is no preparation for them to leave either. The Navy, Army, and Air Force seem to be treating Tianjin as their base. If the increase in the number of troops stationed in North China is approved by the military headquarters, their future movements deserve close attention. (December 15th)

Taiwanese Establish Xiamen Financial Association with Funds Subsidized by the Taiwan Governor-General's Office to Engage in Savings and Mortgage Business 93

Xiamen News: After holding the Tropical Industry Conference and the Overseas Joint Conference in Taiwan, the Japanese have subsequently held the South China Japanese Consular Conference in Hong Kong, which is the beginning of Japan's southern policy. Although the content is secret, the plan is to develop economies in South China and Southeast Asia with Taiwan as the center. The region includes Fujian, Guangdong, Hong Kong, the Philippines, British and Dutch colonies, and Thailand. The business includes expanding the Japanese goods market, promoting shipping, and assisting the economic development of overseas Chinese in these areas. The "Xiamen Financial Association," which recently opened in Xiamen, came into being under this purpose. This organization is hosted by the Japanese Consul in Xiamen under the orders of the Taiwan Governor-General's Office and organized by the Taiwan Public Association. Chen Changfu, the former director of the Taiwan Public Association, is in charge. It opened on December 16th at No. 50 Zhenbang Road. Chen Changfu was elected as the chairman, Shi Fanqi as the standing supervisor, and Su Jiahe, the loan officer of the Taipei China and South Sea Bank, was transferred as the manager. The business executives are Wang Changsheng, Lin Mushi, Cai Jitang, Weng Junming, and 12 others, all outstanding Taiwanese residents in Xiamen. Its business is similar to that of a savings bank, but its lending is similar to that of a commercial bank. The items include savings, loans, guarantees, remittances, chattel loans, mortgages (i.e., acceptance and loan document mortgages), and business asset mortgages. The initial fund is 200,000 yuan, and another 200,000 yuan in low-interest funds are subsidized by the Taiwan Governor-General's Office for the start-up. The initial fund is raised from all parties by the initiators. Each share is 20 yuan, with 5 yuan payable first, and the remaining 15 yuan payable in 15 months. Each person cannot exceed 50 shares, and only those who are economically independent can join. If there are property owners, their wives can also subscribe to shares according to the rules. After the estimated fund is fully raised, those who wish to subscribe to shares will not be restricted. The more shares, the larger the business scale. In the future, branches may be set up in various parts of southern Fujian. It is said that its current business focuses on industrial mortgages. At a time when the local economy is sluggish, finances are tight, and banks have stopped lending, the association is rising to the occasion and doing what others are unwilling to do, so it is attracting attention from the general public. Moreover, the association's business is subject to the supervision of the Japanese Consul in Xiamen, which is a joint venture between Japanese officials and businessmen and is a general partnership. The articles of association have been drafted and sent to the Japanese consulate for review. At the opening ceremony on the 16th, Sakamoto Ryuichi, the chief of the foreign affairs section of the Taiwan Governor-General's Office, happened to be passing through Xiamen, and Yamada Yoshitaro also attended the meeting. Chinese officials who went to congratulate them included Lin Guogeng, the commander of the Xiamen fortress. (December 18th)

Jingdezhen Porcelain Industry Declines, Construction Department Director Requests Relief from the Provincial Government 94

Nanchang News: Jingdezhen porcelain is one of China's special products. It was famous in the Tang and Song dynasties. The West used porcelain as the name for China, which shows its significance. In its heyday, there were 100,000 porcelain workers, and the annual output was always in the thousands and millions of yuan. In recent years, the world market has been squeezed, foreign porcelain has been dumped domestically, and the internal and external economy is in a slump, which has greatly reduced purchasing power. This porcelain, which is famous at home and abroad, is on the verge of collapse. Nearly half of the kiln owners and factories have closed down or suspended operations, and 40 to 50% of the workers are unemployed. Although the local authorities in the province have plans to improve and revitalize it, they are mostly just empty words and have not yet been put into practice. Now, Long Xuesui, the director of the Construction Department of this province, believes that the country's original handicrafts are declining day by day, while large-scale mechanized industries and heavy industries are limited by human resources, financial resources, and the dumping power of foreign goods, and there is no way to develop them in a short time. It is better to improve and revive handicrafts to relieve unemployed masses and dilapidated rural areas. Therefore, during this inspection of the water conservancy construction in Poyang, Leping, Duchang, and other places, he personally went to Jingdezhen for investigation and has now returned to the province. According to reports, Jingdezhen's porcelain industry used to have an output of 10 million yuan, but this year it is less than 2.78 million yuan. Its decline is alarming. If no measures are taken to provide relief, it will become more and more unbearable. Therefore, it has been decided to submit the matter to the provincial government meeting next week to seek urgent relief and permanent solutions. (December 15th)

Zhenjiang Farmers Bank Increases Capital 99

The business of the Jiangsu Provincial Farmers Bank has been very developed in recent years, with annual turnover of several tens of millions of yuan, making it the only institution in the province to provide relief to rural areas. The bank's capital was provisionally set at 2.2 million yuan, based on the farmer bank funds collected from the counties by the end of June of the 20th year of the Republic. In the 23rd year, the provincial government's 637th meeting resolved to allocate Guantian land in Luomahu, Suqian, and appraise it to supplement the bank's funds. Therefore, as of the most recent total, the farmer bank funds collected from the counties, together with the funds allocated by the provincial government, amounted to 4 million yuan. The total amount should be changed to 4 million yuan to reflect the actual situation. The supervisory committee has now submitted this to the Ministry of Finance for record filing, requested the committee to forward the business license No. 110, previously issued by the Ministry of Finance, for cancellation, and requested a new license to be issued.

Xiaoshan Steps to Reorganize County Chamber of Commerce 102

All procedures will be carried out from December 10th to 15th for the first stage, which is to reorganize the internal registration of members, create a membership roster, and record the resumes of staff members, and elect the rosters of officers. The second stage, from December 16th to 28th, is to convene members and responsible personnel of various industry associations to establish industry associations. The third stage, from December 29th to 31st, is the date of establishment of the Chamber of Commerce, revise the articles of association, submit them to the County Party Headquarters for approval, and hold a membership meeting to elect officers.

Bengbu Old Shipyard Bandits Rob Merchant Ships 103

Recently, bandits have been appearing at night in the Old Shipyard area west of Huaiyuan, robbing merchant ships. Hu Yugai, the commander of the 1st Brigade of the Huai River Police, consulted with the Luohe District Office and the Tianjia'an Joint Security Office to determine joint defense and suppression measures, as well as the time and location of the joint patrols, to ensure the safety of merchant ships. He also reported to the long-distance small wheelboats to leave Bengbu early every day, so as to pass through the Old Shipyard no later than 5 PM. If it is after 5 PM, they should stop at Huangtunyao and not move forward to prevent any accidents. The Public Security Bureau believes that the proposed joint defense and suppression measures are appropriate. In addition to instructing them to handle them as proposed, it has recently ordered the public ticket office to comply.

Fudan Students Petitioned at the Municipal Government Yesterday Afternoon, Met with the Mayor and Presented Five Points, Wu Telegraphed Beijing to Release Students 104

Yesterday afternoon at around 2 PM, about two to three hundred students from Fudan University marched to the municipal government to petition. The order was very good. Along the way, they shouted slogans such as "Support the National Government," "Oppose the Puppet Autonomous North China," and other slogans. Upon arriving at the municipal government, they lined up in front of the municipal government's stone steps. Mayor Wu personally received them. Student representatives presented five written requests: 1. Please telegraph to the Beijing authorities to release the arrested students and to compensate the injured students. 2. Guarantee the students' patriotic movement. 3. Punish the officials and military police who oppressed the student movement in Beijing. 4. Oppose the new organization for disguised autonomy in North China. 5. Request the government to issue a clear order to suppress the rebels on a certain date. Mayor Wu immediately gave separate answers and earnestly persuaded them, hoping that the student movement in this city must strictly abide by discipline and maintain order. The students then lined up and returned to school. The original text of Mayor Wu's telegram to the Beijing Municipal Government is copied below: To the Beijing Municipal Government, Today, a petitioning group of students from Fudan University in Shanghai came to the government to petition, requesting a telegram to your government, requesting the immediate release of the arrested students who were petitioning in Beijing, and the injured students to be treated. Please investigate immediately. If true, please release and treat the arrested and injured students separately to be in line with the situation. What to do, and I hope to see a reply. Shanghai Municipal Government.

It is also reported that about five to six thousand students from Jinan, Datong, Jiaotong, Guanghua, Chizhi, Fudan, Taxation College, Nanyang Model Middle School, and others began to assemble and proceed overnight last night, preparing to petition the municipal government this morning.

National Federation of Chambers of Commerce Receives Reply Telegrams from Various Yuan and Ministries 106

Qianku: Agreed on Settlement Procedures; Settlements from Various Zhuang Begin Verification 110

Shiye News Agency reports: The Qian Industry Preparatory Treasury held an executive committee meeting the day before yesterday to discuss the bank settlement procedures and the settlements from various Zhuang. Verification has now begun. The details are as follows:

Agreement on Settlement

The Shanghai Qian Industry United Preparatory Treasury, affiliated with the Qian Industry Association, in view of the imminent bank settlement period and the approaching final settlement for the industry, specially convened the third executive committee meeting in the conference room of the treasury on Ningbo Road at 3:00 PM the day before yesterday. Attendees included He Zhongxiao, Xi Jiming, Liu Wuqiao, Shao Yanshan, Lu Shuchen, Zhang Mengzhou, Chen Lishan, Wang Jimei, Zhao Songyuan, Shen Jingliang, Qin Runqing, Li Shoushan, Xie Taofu, Pei Yunqing, Sheng Xiaoshan, and fifteen others. Qin Xieqing, the general manager of the Qianku, was present as an observer. Chairman He Zhongxiao reported on the content of the meeting, the Qianku reserve fund, and the accounts of various Zhuang. There was careful discussion of the various procedures for bank settlement, which concluded at approximately 4:00 PM.

Beginning of Verification

The Qianku is the central hub for the Qian industry, both internally and externally. The bank settlements received by various banks must be handed over to the clearing house representative to transfer to the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications. The bank settlements received by various Qian Zhuang must be handed over to the Qianku representative to transfer to the three banks. The transactions are smooth and without any errors. Now that the Qianku believes that the Qian industry's accounts with the banks should be clearly verified, it has, based on the decision of the third executive committee meeting, notified all affiliated Zhuang yesterday to quickly send to the treasury a detailed verification of their accounts with the banks and transactions with other firms for the past year, in order to facilitate settlement with the various banks. At the same time, it will concentrate the current funds and total all temporary reserve funds of various Zhuang, in order to consolidate the foundation. Regarding loans from various Zhuang, it has been decided that starting next month, they will begin to be recovered or have interest settled and rolled over.

International Wireless Telephone: Initial Sino-French Test; Results Good, but Voice Still Lacking Clarity 111

Shenshi News Agency reports: The International Telecommunications Bureau of the Ministry of Communications and the International Radio Station are preparing for international telephone service. In the past two days, they conducted test calls with Paris, France, at the Liuheng Radio Station, with good results. The test calls were made using the second telephone set, which had just been installed. The station's chief engineer, together with a British engineer from the International Telecommunications Bureau, jointly opened the test and conducted it smoothly. However, due to the significant distance between China and France in terms of longitude and latitude, the voice was still lacking clarity. However, testing is still ongoing. According to the International Radio Station, the most difficult aspect of the Sino-French telephone test is the significant time difference, which makes the preparation process time-consuming. Although test calls have now begun with the other country, the time difference is as much as seven hours, which is greater than the time difference with the UK, causing inconvenience to both parties. The station has decided to make every effort to plan and ensure that the time for both parties is appropriately coordinated.

Xu Shiying Went to Beijing Yesterday to Meet with the New President Chiang 113

Xu Shiying, Chairman of the Central Relief Committee and Vice-Chairman of the Shanghai Fundraising Association for Flood Victims in Various Provinces, recently, due to the reorganization of the central government, should have requested to resign from his position. However, the new President Chiang believes that Mr. Xu has been handling relief affairs for many years and has made great contributions. The central government relies on him greatly and could not allow him to retire immediately. He specially proposed this matter at the first meeting of the Executive Yuan, and after discussion, it was decided to retain him. Mr. Xu then stated that relief affairs were complicated, and he personally felt exhausted. He urgently requested the central government to appoint other capable individuals so that he could rest. Furthermore, the severe winter has arrived, and the flood victims in various provinces are suffering from hunger and cold, which is unbearable to witness. The issue of planting in the coming spring cannot be ignored. Before he is completely relieved of his duties, he should find a way to provide fundamental relief to prevent tens of millions of disaster victims from perishing or resorting to desperate measures. Therefore, at 1:30 PM yesterday, he took the Beijing-Zhabei express train to Beijing to meet with President Chiang and request a solution and to personally request his resignation from the position of Chairman of the Relief Committee again. He will return to Shanghai in about three to five days.

Shanghai Chinese Ratepayers' Association Sends Letter to the Shanghai Municipal Council Requesting Maximum Reduction of Expenses and Deletion of All Non-Essential Expenditures, and Immediate Adoption of Vacant House and Land Tax 114

The Shanghai Chinese Ratepayers' Association sent a letter yesterday to Mr. Zhong Siyun, Director-General of the Shanghai Municipal Council, stating: "Having read the summary report on the financial situation by the Director of the Treasury of your council, it is clear that the economic situation of businesses and residents in the Shanghai International Settlement is declining, which is affecting the income from property tax and licenses. This situation cannot be changed overnight. Therefore, the only way for your council to plan its finances in the future is to reduce expenses as much as possible. For example, when hiring staff, Chinese employees with equal ability but lower salaries should be employed. Non-essential expenditures such as music bands should be deleted. The goal is to adapt to the living standards of the citizens. Actions that are akin to draining the pond to catch all the fish, such as overestimating property tax and increasing license fees, will not only fail to benefit revenue but will also accelerate the collapse of the market. They should be strictly stopped to nurture the tax base. Furthermore, this association has repeatedly sent letters to your council advocating the collection of vacant land and house tax, which is necessary for immediate adoption."

Officials and Businessmen Call for Relief for Industry and Finance Through Reduced Interest Rates and Inclusion of Land Deeds in Bond Reserves; Three Banks Ordered to Gradually Implement Inclusion of Land Deeds in Bond Reserves 116

The Ministry of Finance has ordered the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications to gradually implement reduced interest rates in the market based on the social and economic situation. The Qian industry has requested the Supervisory Committee and the three banks to reduce the interest on loans. The Chamber of Commerce has submitted a request to the Ministry to allow land deeds to be included in bond reserves. Details are as follows:

Reduction of Interest Rates Ordered to Be Implemented

Leaders of the industrial sector, Yu Qiaqing, Liu Hongsheng, Guo Xu, Rong Zongjing, Nie Lusheng, and others, met with Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi to request that the government quickly establish a special bank or first have the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications allocate a large sum of money to relieve industry, so that entrepreneurs can fully utilize their capital. They also requested the Central Bank to reduce interest rates in the market and find ways to recover high-interest bonds to encourage the general public to invest in industry. Yesterday, a reporter from the Xin Sheng News Agency learned from banking circles that the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications have already implemented overdrafts and interbank lending for the same industry, which indirectly relieves industry and commerce. The Real Estate Mortgage Bank is being planned by the Ministry of Finance and is scheduled to be established next spring. Regarding the reduction of interest rates in the market, the Ministry of Finance has instructed the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications to gradually implement this based on the social and economic situation. The three banks have now been ordered to comply.

Qian Industry Requests Three Banks to Reduce Interest

The Ministry of Finance previously allocated 25 million yuan in financial bonds in 1935 to relieve the Qian industry and organized the Qian Industry Supervisory Committee. The Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications were responsible for 18 million yuan, and various commercial banks jointly committed 4 million yuan. The funds from the Qian Industry Preparatory Treasury and various commercial banks have been repaid in full. However, more than 17 million yuan from the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications has not yet been repaid. Now, the Ministry of Finance and the three banks have agreed to temporarily postpone repayment. Yesterday, a reporter from the Xin Sheng News Agency learned from Qian industry circles that various borrowing Qian Zhuang have jointly requested the Qian Industry Supervisory Committee to forward a request to the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications to appropriately reduce the long-term interest rate of 8% on these relief loans. It is reported that the committee has forwarded the request to the three banks for consideration.

Land Deeds Included in Bond Reserves

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce submitted a request to the Ministry of Finance yesterday, stating: "Regarding the request to submit a report, on the 17th of this month, we received a letter from the Shanghai Land Bureau stating that, according to the Ministry of Finance's implementation of the new currency policy, various banks use 60% cash and 40% securities as guarantees for exchanging legal tender. If land certificates or land deeds are included in this 40% guarantee, it will further increase the credibility of legal tender and promote the circulation of funds. The economic and financial source of this city largely depends on real estate, just as South Africa depends on gold and Southeast Asia depends on rubber, without any difference. Therefore, to develop the economic and financial source of South Africa and Southeast Asia, it is necessary to promote the circulation and sales of gold and rubber. Similarly, to develop the economic and financial source of Shanghai, it is necessary to promote the circulation of real estate. The situation is the same. Now, with the implementation of the new currency policy, using 60% cash and 40% guarantees to exchange legal tender will invisibly increase the credibility of legal tender. However, the economic and financial source of Shanghai is largely in real estate, as mentioned above. Furthermore, our country has always been a country with import surpluses, and in international trade, it is a debtor country. Funds should flow out of the country. However, in the past few years, the circulation of real estate in Shanghai was high, and land prices were high. The funds obtained by foreign companies importing goods were more profitable by investing in real estate in Shanghai than by remitting them back to their own countries. Therefore, although there was an import surplus, funds did not flow out, and some even remitted their funds stored in their own countries to Shanghai to invest in real estate, which increased the inflow of foreign capital. However, in the past year or two, due to the imperfection of the real estate system, the real estate economy has collapsed. In addition to the draft of the Shanghai City Implementation of Land Practice Certificate Mortgage Rights Regulations and actively reorganizing and improving various businesses of the Land Bureau, we believe that to restore the economic and financial situation of a few years ago and increase the credibility of legal tender, it is necessary to include real estate as a guarantee for exchanging legal tender. In this way, it will not only have the above-mentioned effects on foreign capital, but also make the funds in the interior more active due to investment in real estate. Moreover, landowners are the backbone of society and the economy. If land certificates or land deeds can be used as guarantees for exchanging legal tender, they will naturally have a deep and close relationship of interests, thereby increasing the credibility of legal tender. If only stocks and bonds are listed as guarantees for exchanging legal tender, only a small number of merchants and industrialists who are smaller than landowners will gain credibility for legal tender. If the majority and powerful landowners are omitted, it seems that the development of the economic and financial source and the increase of the credibility of legal tender will not be complete. Furthermore, most merchants and industrialists are also landowners. Including land certificates or land deeds as guarantees for exchanging legal tender is even more desirable for them. As evidenced by previous examples, Germany also used land resources as guarantees to issue banknotes after the European War. It is not an accidental fact that they also saw this. Therefore, there is a considerable basis for habits and principles. Considering the social and economic situation and referring to the German precedent, we believe that it is necessary to include land certificates or land deeds as guarantees for exchanging legal tender. In addition to submitting a request to the Municipal Government to forward it to the Ministry of Finance for consideration, we are presenting our views and hopes that they will be adopted and consistently advocated. Sincerely hope." Upon arrival, this matter was presented to your ministry on March 13 of this year, proposing five measures to relieve the market, requesting that they be adopted. In the second measure, it was mentioned that deeds and land practice certificates should be included as guarantees for bond reserves under the Central Bank. Subsequently, the Ministry of Finance issued a reply with the number Qian Zi 5402, stating that it was feared that the proportion occupied would be too large, and if there was an emergency, it would be difficult to realize. The request should not be discussed. It can be seen that your ministry has carefully considered and planned comprehensively. However, the monetary system is now slightly different from the past. Therefore, if the proportion of land deeds is appropriately increased in the guarantee reserve, it does not seem to be a major obstacle. Based on the previous letter, we are preparing a document to submit to your ministry for review, requesting that it be adopted and implemented.

Tobacco Exchange Association Resolves to Ban Private Hoarding of Silver Coins; Will Submit to This Year's General Meeting for Discussion and Decision 117

City Chamber of Commerce Announces the Process of Blocking the Sale of Liujiang Coal; The Chamber of Commerce Advocates Suing for Receiving Stolen Goods 118

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, based on the report from the Liujiang Coal Mine Railway Company that the Zhongfu Company was promoting stolen coal from the Taiji Company, helping to commit crimes, and ordered a firm notice to all members that they must not sell the coal. If anyone is greedy for private gain and disregards the law, the Chamber of Commerce and the Coal Industry Association should impose severe sanctions. Yesterday, the Chamber of Commerce announced the handling of the situation as follows:

Process of Blocking the Sale of Stolen Coal from Taiji

On October 23 of this year, the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce received a letter from the Chinese-owned Liujiang Coal Mine Company, stating that the Taiji Company illegally occupied the mining area by force and requested that justice be upheld, and that all industries refuse to buy the above-mentioned mine coal. The Chamber of Commerce replied that since the Liujiang Company had filed a lawsuit according to law, the illegally mined and sold coal should be stopped. The key to this matter is entirely in the coal industry. The decision is to rotate the industry. Other industries mostly have less contact with the coal industry. The Liujiang Company has already sent letters to the coal and rotating industries, requesting their assistance. The handling has been effective. If the company believes that it is necessary to notify other industries, it can notify them of the names and addresses listed in the Chamber of Commerce membership directory.

Correspondence with Zhongfu Company

On December 9 of this year, the Liujiang Coal Mine Company sent a letter to the Chamber of Commerce, stating: "Our company's mining area was previously illegally occupied by force by the Taiji Company, and the stored coal was transported to Shanghai for sale. On October 21 of this year, we sent a letter to your association requesting assistance. At the same time, our company sent a letter to the Coal Industry Association, refusing to buy and sell, and published a statement requesting attention from all sectors. No matter what name the Taiji Company uses to transport the coal to Shanghai, do not be fooled into promoting or selling it on their behalf to avoid disputes. Now it is seen in the newspaper that Hebei white coal is being sold under the name of Zhongfu Company. It is heard that the company is organized by your committee member, Mr. Ma Shaoquan. The so-called Hebei white coal is the Liujiang coal transported from our company's mining area to Shanghai and stored in Pudong. Our company believes that Mr. Ma's personality and status would not lead to this. However, since there are rumors, we would like to request that your association ask Mr. Ma to make a statement to dispel doubts." After receiving the letter, the Chamber of Commerce immediately forwarded it to Mr. Ma Shaoquan on the 9th, requesting him to investigate and reply. On December 10, Mr. Ma Shaoquan replied to the Chamber of Commerce, stating: "I received your letter, stating that the Liujiang Coal Mine Company and the Coal Industry Association have entrusted me to investigate the Zhongfu Company's sale of Hebei white coal, and that the organization is set up by me. What mine in Hebei is the coal from? Please investigate and reply. I have not organized any organization to sell Hebei white coal. However, I heard that my relative, Ma Zhaoye, has invested capital in the so-called Zhongfu Company. If the association wants to know the details of this matter, please inquire directly with Mr. Ma Zhaoye." The Chamber of Commerce then forwarded the letter to Ma Zhaoye of the Zhongfu Company, requesting him to reply with the details as soon as possible. Then, on the 11th, it received a letter from Ma Zhaoye of the Zhongfu Company, stating: "Regarding this case, our company received a letter of questioning from the Liujiang Company on the 8th of this month. We replied that our company has its own cargo owner to contact us for the sale of Hebei white coal. There is no need to inform us of the details you inquired about. Our company has not commented on the various disputes with others. The Hebei coal of our company is sold as an agent through legal procedures, just like the coal currently sold by the coal industry, such as Kishima, Matsuura, Miike, Fushun, Jilin, Kaohsiung, Kantou, etc. All these types of coal have been sold for a long time, and we have never heard of any objections from the industry. Therefore, there should be no discrimination against our company's sale of Hebei white coal." After receiving the letter, the City Chamber of Commerce forwarded the information to Liujiang Coal Mine Company and the Coal Industry Association.
